		var force = '';
		var ignore = '';

      <div class="post-4608 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-satellite-tv-tutorials tag-2476 tag-2477 tag-43-are-off tag-ss9e tag-swa-are-not-showing tag-why-code-40 tag-why-ss8 entry">
       <h1 class="entry-title">
        Reasons Why Some Qsat Are Offline, While Some Channels are Off &amp; Other Issues
       </h1>
       <div class="post-info">
        <span class="date published time" title="2014-08-05T05:38:16+00:00">
         August 5, 2014
        </span>
        By
        <span class="author vcard">
         <span class="fn">
          <a href="http://www.lemmymorgan.com/author/lemmymorgan/" rel="author">
           lemmy
          </a>
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="post-comments">
         <a href="http://www.lemmymorgan.com/reasons-why-some-qsat-are-offline-while-some-channels-are-off-other-issues/#comments">
          260 Comments
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <script id="mNCC" language="javascript">
        medianet_width='300';  medianet_height= '250';  medianet_crid='580437677';
       </script>
       <script id="mNSC" language="javascript" src="http://contextual.media.net/nmedianet.js?cid=8CU4M6T8K">
       </script>
       <div class="entry-content">
        <p>
         Am hereby combining all the basic (confusing) questions some qsat users ask, with a view to providing convincing answers to them once and for all. I will love to go straight to the point without much ado. Please take your time to read in between the lines and you will surely get the gist.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://i2.wp.com/lemmymorgan.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/qsat_instability.jpg">
          <img alt="qsat_instability" class="aligncenter wp-image-4609 size-full" data-recalc-dims="1" src="http://i2.wp.com/lemmymorgan.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/qsat_instability.jpg?resize=275%2C183"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="color: #0000ff;">
          <strong>
           Question:
          </strong>
         </span>
         Why my qsat not showing any Scrambled channels on (D s t v)While that of My Neighbor is working fine?
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Ans:
         </strong>
         This is most likely caused by server problems by qsat team. the server problems is also caused by overloading a server due to massive sales. Some qsat on certain ports will have to go off till they resolve the issue. in some instances, qsat team may release new software to correct the issue, however in 98% of the such occurrence, all qsat that are offline are auto restored within a period of not more than 7days(at time it could be two days, three days e.t.c)
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="color: #0000ff;">
          <strong>
           Question:
          </strong>
         </span>
         How Do I know my qsat is having a specific server problems instead of a general down-times of all qsat?
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Ans:
         </strong>
         First of all, you must make sure you have not modified either your qsat or your internet protocol on qsat, in other words, your qsat was previously working fine, and you have a valid account. Also, you must have upgraded to the latest qsat software which is v6.52 o Next watch out for the following symptoms; Your qsat will display the usual Network Connection Success, Your qsat will be able to view your account expiry and avatarcam codes, your qsat will note give you the usual Welcome to server your account remain . days message, In some instances, you may not even be able to view your account expiry, you must have asked from another qsat user or your local satellite installer to know whether qsat is off generally or not, Your avatarcam code will include the following which varies with time; code
         <em>
          <strong>
           40***, 41***&lt; 42***, 43***, 59(on rare occasions), 57***(on rare occasions), 45***(very rare occasions). T
          </strong>
         </em>
         he solution is for you to watch and pray that qsat teams solves the problem fast enough and trust me, if your problem can be solve through a new software, you will be able to download one here. But in 99% of the casse, you only need to wait till it start working back by itself. If your code is not mentioned above, and yet your qsat is not showing, it means your case is similar to the one above.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <span style="color: #0000ff;">
           Question:
          </span>
         </strong>
         Why is my qsat freezing so badly with my good internet connection?
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Ans:
         </strong>
         As long as you are not using a sim card directly, then it is due to qsat server please dont modify your device. however, if you are using a sim card, please change the sim card, or better still change to a 3g modem. But if your internet is perfectly ok, then it is server problem from qsat. In fact when yours is freezing, some qsat out there are totally offline.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <span style="color: #0000ff;">
           Question:
          </span>
         </strong>
         Why are the following channels not showing on qsat; ss8, swa, ss9e?
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Ans:
         </strong>
         As for ss9e and swa, i dont know why it is not showing on qsat because they are showing on tv1 cccam account. though those channels are meant for east and south Africans with position 68,0E.
         <strong>
          you cant receive ss8 in Nigeria because it is not for west africans
         </strong>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <span style="color: #0000ff;">
           Question:
          </span>
         </strong>
         Why are all HD channels not showing? Or why did HD channels No longer opening on Qsat?
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Ans:
         </strong>
         Well the best answer to this is that; if it is easy for qsat to open HD channels, they will kindly do so because they have done it before. ASit stands, no account or decoder in africa is currently capable of opening any HD channels on dst*. So please forget about HD channels for now, and be content with SD channels. Meanwhile, if you must watch HD channels, then buy speed HD decoder, it opens all channel on canalsat both SD and HD(canalsat is a french satellite provider with few english channels but thise few English channels are not HD)
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <span style="color: #0000ff;">
           Question:
          </span>
         </strong>
         Why has french channels like Can+S, RTL9 and some indian channels stopped working on Qsat on D S T V frequency?
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Ans:
         </strong>
         well ever since qsat introduced speed hd s1 for french speaking African counties, they disabled all french channels on dst* frequency however i dont know why some india channels are not showing. Tv1 cccam account still shows all french channels and most india channels on dst* frequency.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <span style="color: #0000ff;">
           Question:
          </span>
         </strong>
         Why is only few channels showing on My qsat? for example ss3 is not showing at all
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Ans:
         </strong>
         This may be caused by dst* upgrade or qsat internal server problem. Be that as it may, the missing channels will be back(all other things being equal)
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <span style="color: #0000ff;">
           Question:
          </span>
         </strong>
         I have iptv menu on my qsat q23g, but i cant find dqiptv menu, I need the software to enable dqiptv menu on q23g.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Ans:
         </strong>
         Am afraid, qsat q23g doenst come with dqiptv menu by default, and as at the time of writing this post, there is no software available out there that could add dqiptv menu to qsat q23g. If sometimes in the future such software is released, i will inform the house.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <span style="color: #0000ff;">
           Question:
          </span>
         </strong>
         Is avatarcam code the same as a cccam account?
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Ans:
         </strong>
         Capital No. avatarcam is the preloaded, inbuilt account / code that comes with your qsat and it is valid for one year starting from the day you activate the qsat. Cccam on the other hand, is an independent account, managed on a separated server from qsat, but can be used with qsat as a backup / alternative
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Conclusion
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         The above post was the best i could remember, if you are having a question not contained above, please make use of the comment box below to ask your question. For now, feel free to share this article to your friends
        </p>

          <div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
           <a href="http://www.lemmymorgan.com/reasons-why-some-qsat-are-offline-while-some-channels-are-off-other-issues/#comment-39020">
            August 15, 2014 at 8:07 pm
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="comment-content">
          <p>
           My Q23g is now opening and  showing dst* channels very well and clear. A friend told me to change my sim card to Airtel, switch off the receiver, switch on to boot, blind scan dst* channels, off the receiver, switch on again to boot. Leave it for some minutes until it displays expiry date. Then it open all dst* channels. Mine is working now. Good luck.
          </p>
         </div>
